msg:I have stayed at many Crown Plaza hotels, so I probably know its facilities and service levels. I have never been too surprised, but this time I was pleasantly surprised!
Convenient location: The hotel has a direct bus stop from Hong Kong. It is a 5-minute walk to the Zumiao MTR Station, and 10 minutes to the Zumiao and Lingnan Tiandi. It is more convenient than imagined.
Considerate service: It was my birthday when I checked in. In addition to saying happy birthday, the front desk manager also unexpectedly upgraded my room to a suite. After I checked in, I found a small birthday cake on the table. He moved so quickly and was very nice. Heartwarming.
Complete facilities: In addition to the swimming pool and fitness room, the hotel also has a spa and massage. The environment is comfortable, the technicians have authentic techniques, and the charges are reasonable. In addition, there are guest discounts, which are not at all like hotel charges.
Rich breakfast: The buffet breakfast is available for a long time, from 6:30 to 10:30, with a wide variety of options. In addition to Chinese and Western breakfast, Cantonese dim sum (even served from a dim sum cart), and even Indian food, there is always something to suit your taste. !
I am very satisfied with this experience and will definitely stay here next time I come back.
